samewarmeo da gakotrebis saqmeTa palata

davis sagani:


fuladi valdebulebis Sesruleba (ZiriTad da Sege-


bebul sarCelebSi).


aRwerilobiTi nawili:


2001w. 1 maiss ss `saqtransgazmrewvis~ warmomadgenelma b. kviri-


kaSvilma sarCeli aRZra sasamarTlosi ss `saqarTvelos gazis saer-


TaSoriso korporaciis~ mimarT da moiTxova xelSekrulebis darRve-


viT gamowveuli zianis anazRaureba 8502097,14 laris odenobiT.


mosarCelem ganmarta, rom 1999w. 9 dekembers ss `saqtransgazmrew-


vsa~ da ss `saqarTvelos gazis saerTaSoriso korporacias~ Soris dai-


do xelSekruleba saqarTvelos magistraluri gazsadenebis sistemis


momsaxurebaze, romlis vada ganisazRvra 2000w. 9 ivnisamde Semdgomi


prolongaciiT. xelSekrulebis sagans warmoadgenda ss `saqtransgaz-


mrewvis~ mier gazis momxmarebelTa Seuferxebeli da usafrTxo gazmo-


maragebis uzrunvelsayofad korporaciis kuTvnili magistraluri


gazsadenebis sistemis teqnikuri momsaxureba. ss `saqtransgazmrewvma~


Seasrula xelSekrulebiT nakisri valdebulebebi magistraluri gaz-


sadenis sistemis momsaxurebis Taobaze, rasac adasturebs gazis tran-


sportirebis teqnikuri balansi da rasac mopasuxe sadavod ar xdis.


amave xelSekrulebis 4.1. punqtiT mopasuxe ss `saqarTvelos gazis saer-


TaSoriso korporacias~ ekisreboda ss `saqtransgazmrewvisTvis~ ma-


gistraluri sistemis momsaxurebaze Sesrulebuli samuSaoebis Rire-


bulebis anazRaurebis valdebuleba. xelSekrulebiT nakisri valdebu-


lebis Seusruleblobis Sedegad mopasuxes ss `saqtransgazmrewvis~ mi-

davalianeba, xolo 3879925,5 lars _ masze daricxuli sauravi.

sabuRaltro eqspertizis daskvniT ss `saqtransgazmrewvis~ mier


gaweuli momsaxurebis Rirebuleba Seadgens 3884198,40 lars. mopasu-


xe korporaciam am valis arseboba aRiara. Sesabamisad, sasamarTlom


ixelmZRvanela ssk-is 131-e muxliT, romlis Tanaxmad, erTi mxaris mi-

Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos kolegiis gadawyvetilebaze saka-


sacio saCivari Seitana ss `saqtransgazmrewvma~, romliTac moiTxova


gasaCivrebuli gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba, axali gadawyvetilebiT sa-


sarCelo moTxovnis srulad dakmayofileba da Segebebul sarCelze


uaris Tqma Semdeg garemoebaTa gamo:


1. gadawyvetileba kanonis darRveviTaa gamotanili, radganac sasa-


marTlom ar gamoiyena kanoni, romelic unda gamoeyenebina, daarRvia


ssk-is normebi, ris Sedegadac saqmeze miRebul iqna araswori gadawyve-


tileba, kerZod, sasamarTlom saqme ganixila mosarCele mxaris monawi-


2643


leobis gareSe, romelsac ar miuRia Setyobineba kanoniT dadgenili


wesiT. sasamarTlom ugulebelyo ssk-is 70-e muxlis moTxovna, romlis


Tanaxmad, mxareebsa da maTs warmomadgenlebs sasamarTlo uwyebiT ec-


nobebaT sasamarTlo sxdomis calkeuli saproceso moqmedebis Sesru-


lebis dro da adgili. radgan aRniSnuli norma aris imperatiuli, sasa-


marTlo valdebuli iyo sasamarTlo Setyobinebebi gaegzavna ss `saq-


transgazmrewvis~ warmomadgenlebisTvis, rac ar gaukeTebia. Sedegad,


maT ver SeZles sasamarTlo procesSi monawileobis miReba da marwmu-


neblis interesebis dacva. sasamarTlom yovelgvari safuZvlis gareSe


ar gaiTvaliswina is garemoeba, rom mosarCelis warmomadgeneli b.kvi-


rikaSvili 2004w. 19 Tebervals, dRis 11 saaTidan monawileobda didu-


be-CuRureTis raionul sasamarTlosi sisxlis samarTlis saqmis gan-


xilvaSi. aRniSnuli garemoebebi, ssk-is 241-e muxlisa da 394-e muxlis


`b~ qvepunqtis Tanaxmad, gadawyvetilebis gauqmebis safuZvelia.


vinaidan gadawyvetileba gamotanil iqna mosarCelis dauswreb-


lad, 229-e muxlis Tanaxmad, sasamarTlo valdebuli iyo mopasuxis


Suamdgomlobis safuZvelze gamoetana dauswrebeli gadawyvetileba,


xolo Tu mopasuxe amas ar moiTxovda, sasamarTlos unda gamoetana


ganCineba sarCelis ganuxilvelad datovebis Sesaxeb. mosarCele mxa-


ris monawileobis gareSe sasamarTlos mier daswrebuli gadawyveti-


lebis gamotaniT saxezea saproceso normebis uxeSi darRveva da pro-


cesualuri Seusabamoba. saproceso kanonmdeblobiT daswrebuli da


dauswrebeli gadawyvetilebis gamotanis sruliad sxvadasxva proce-


sualuri wesebia dadgenili da, amdenad, Tu sasamarTlo dauswrebel


gadawyvetilebas gamoitanda, misi gauqmebis yvelanairi samarTleb-


rivi safuZveli gaaCndaT. daswrebuli gadawyvetilebis gamotaniT ki


sasamarTlom xelovnurad SeuzRuda mosarCeles gadawyvetilebis


gauqmebis erT-erTi samarTlebrivi safuZveli.


2. gadawyvetileba iuridiulad dausabuTebelia da dasabuTeba im-


denad arasrulia, rom gadawyvetilebis samarTlebrivi safuZvlia-


nobis Semowmeba SeuZlebelia. sasamarTlo Tavis gadawyvetilebaSi


saerTod ar uTiTebs im samarTlebriv normebs, romlebsac daafuZna


gadawyvetileba. sasamarTlom yovelgvari motivirebuli safuZvle-


bis gareSe ar moaxdina saqmeSi arsebuli sabuRaltro eqspertizis


daskvnis analizi da yovelgvari dasabuTebis gareSe gaiziara igi. ro-


gor eqspertizis daskvnaSi, ise sasamarTlos gadawyvetilebaSi ar


aris dasabuTebuli da argumentirebuli gaangariSebis is finansuri


da samarTlebrivi kriteriumebi, rac gaxda gadawyvetilebaSi miTi-


Tebuli Tanxebis dakisrebis safuZveli. arasworia sasamarTlos mier


gaziarebuli eqspertizis daskvnis is nawili, sadac gazis transpor-


tirebis normirebul danakargad miCneulia 5,07%, xolo gazis sabi-


Tumo sarealizacio fasad _ 140 lari. mocemul SemTxvevaSi normire-


2644


bul danakargad miCneul unda yofiliyo 6,8%, xolo sarealizacio


fasad _ 123,9 lari. gadawyvetilebaSi araferia naTqvami imis Sesaxeb,


Tu ra aris sasarCelo moTxovnis mTlian dakmayofilebaze uaris


Tqmis safuZveli, aseve, Tu ratom da ra kriteriumebiT ar miiRo da


uaryo sasamarTlom ZiriTad Tanxaze sauravis daricxva.


sasamarTlom ar gamoiyena kanoni, romelic unda gamoeyenebina,


kerZod, ssk-is me-5, 316-e, 317-e, 361-e, 327-e, 394-e, 403-e, 411-e da 414-e


muxlebi.


ss `saqarTvelos gazis saerTaSoriso korporacia~ sakasacio sa-


Civarze Tavis SepasuxebebSi miuTiTebs, rom sasamarTlo sxdomis


dro cnobili iyo rogorc mosarCelisTvis, ise misi warmomadgenle-


bisTvisac, maT Soris, b.kvirikaSvilisTvis, romelmac moiTxova kide-


vac saqmis ganxilvis gadadeba. ssk-is 71-e muxlis Tanaxmad, sasamar-


Tlo uwyeba dasabarebel pirs unda Cabardes mxaris mier miTiTebul


misamarTze, rac faqtobrivad ganaxorciela sasamarTlom. arc erTi


warmomadgenlis misamarTi sasamarTlosTvis cnobili ar iyo da bu-


nebrivia, uwyebebi igzavneboda saqmeSi miTiTebul mosarCelis iuri-


diul misamarTze. kasatori arasworad miuTiTebs ssk-is 316-e, 317-e,


361-e, 327-e muxlebis darRvevaze, vinaidan aRniSnuli muxlebi ar


ukavSirdeba gansaxilvel davas.


samotivacio nawili:


sakasacio palatam ganixila saqmis masalebi, sakasacio saCivris


safuZvlebi, moismina mxareTa axsna-ganmartebani da Tvlis, rom saka-


sacio saCivari unda dakmayofildes Semdeg garemoebaTa gamo:


palata Tvlis, rom Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos samoqalaqo da


samewarmeo saqmeTa kolegiis gasaCivrebuli gadawyvetileba miRebu-


lia ssk-is moTxovnaTa darRveviT.


ssk-is 70-e muxlis pirveli nawilis Tanaxmad, mxareebs da maT war-


momadgenlebs sasamarTlo uwyebiT ecnobebaT sasamarTlo sxdomis


dro da adgili. aRniSnuli muxli Seicavs rogorc mxaris, aseve misi


warmomadgenlis gafrTxilebis erTnair pirobebs. rogorc saqmis ma-


salebiT irkveva, ss `saqtransgazmrewvis~ warmomadgenels mocemuli


muxlis Sesabamisad sasamarTlo uwyeba ar Cabarebia. palata ver gai-


ziarebs mowinaaRmdege mxaris arguments imis Taobaze, rom ss `saq-


transgazmrewvs~ ar miuTiTebia misi warmomadgenlis misamarTi. ro-


gorc sasarCelo gancxadebaSi, aseve saqmeSi arsebul masalebSi miTi-


Tebulia ss `saqtransgazmrewvs~ warmomadgenlis b.kvirikaSvilis bi-


nis misamarTi, romelzec sasamarTlo uwyeba gagzavnili ar aris.


ssk-is 394-e muxlis `b~ qvepunqtis Tanaxmad, gadawyvetilebis ka-


nonis darRvviT miRebulad cnobis absolutur safuZvels warmoad-


gens sasamarTlos mier saqmis ganxilva erT-erTi mxaris dauswreb-


2645


lad, romelsac ar miuRia Setyobineba kanoniT dadgenili wesiT an mi-


si kanonieri warmomadgenlis gareSe. mocemul SemTxvevaSi palata


Tvlis, rom mosarCele gafrTxilebuli ar aris ssk-is 70-e muxlis Se-


sabamisad, radgan, rogorc ukve aRvniSneT, mocemuli muxli Seicavs


mxaris, aseve misi warmomadgenlis gafrTxilebis kumulaciur piro-


bas, rac sasamarTlos mier daculi ar aris.


unda aRiniSnos is garemoebac, rom ssk-is 233-e muxli krZalavs sa-


samarTlos mier dauswrebeli gadawyvetilebis miRebis SesaZleblo-


bas im SemTxvevaSi, Tu mxare gafrTxilebuli ar aris ssk-is 70-78-e


muxlis Sesabamisad. aRniSnuli muxlis me-2 nawilSi calsaxadaa dad-


genili mosamarTlis moqmedebis farglebi, rac gamoixateba sasamar-


Tlo saqmis ganxilvis sxva droisaTvis gadaniSvnaSi, ris Sesaxebac


unda ecnobos gamoucxadebel mxares da saqmeSi monawile sxva pirebs.


aRniSnulidan gamomdinare, sasamarTlo moklebulia SesaZleblobas


miTiTebuli faqtoris arsebobis SemTxvevaSi saqmeze saerTod mii-


Ros gadawyvetileba. amdenad, gaziarebuli ver iqneba mowinaaRmdege


mxaris mosazreba imis Taobaze, rom saolqo sasamarTlos mier zemoT


miTiTebul darRvevebs ar gamouwvevia araswori gadawyvetilebis mi-


Reba, radgan mocemul SemTxvevaSi sasamarTlo saerTod moklebuli


iyo gadawyvetilebis miRebis SesaZleblobas.


vinaidan kasatorma ramodenimejer Secvala sakasacio saCivris


moTxovna, xolo sabolood moiTxova saqmeze pirveli instanciis sa-

daubrundes imave sasamarTlos.

si bina, magram iq sacxovreblad ar gadadis.

gistraciidan moxsna da binidan gamosaxleba.

2003w. 17 maisis Cuqebis xelSekrulebis baTilad cnoba. man aRniSna,


rom sadavo bina gaformebuli iyo m. dalaqiSvilis saxelze, romel-


sac fsiqikuri mdgomareobis gamo, ar SeeZlo ra mieRo realuri ga-


dawyvetileba, m. dalaqiSvilma mas daSinebiT gaaformebina Cuqebis


xelSekruleba.

dam aCuqa mas bina, vinaidan r. dalaqiSvili mas yuradRebas ar aqcevda.

rulebis gaformebisas araviTar zewolas m. dalaqiSvilis mxridan


adgili ar hqonda da moiTxova r.dalaqiSvilis binidan gamosaxleba.

tors saqmis faqtobrivi garemoebebis dadgenis Taobaze sakasacio


pretenzia (saqmis faqtobrivi garemoebebis dadgena saproceso nor-


mebis darRveviT) ar ganucxadebia.


palata, dadgenili garemoebebis gaTvaliswinebiT, ar iziarebs ka-

da axali gadawyvetilebiT ar dakmayofilda o. wereTlis sarCeli.

mopasuxem sarCeli ar cno im motiviT, rom mosarCeles sadavo bi-


na gadaeca valSi, romlis gadaxdazec igi uars arasodes acxadebda.


baTumis saqalaqo sasamarTlos 2004w. 23 ianvris gadawyvetilebis


a.efimovis sarCeli dakmayofilda.

lumiSvilis saapelacio saCivari, ucvlelad darCa am saqmeze saqala-


qo sasamarTlos gadawyvetileba.


saapelacio palatam dadgenilad cno, rom 2003w. 30 maiss gamocxa-


debul auqcionze sadavo bina sajaro vaWrobis wesiT SeiZina a.efi-


movma, romelic sajaro reestrSi aRiricxa am binis mesakuTred. sk-is


170-e da 172-e muxlebis gamoyenebiT, saapelacio palatam miiCnia, rom


mosarCeles, rogorc mesakuTres, ufleba aqvs, mflobels mosTxovos


nivTis ukan dabruneba, a.mazlumiSvilis ki ar gaaCnia sadavo binis


flobis ufleba. saapelacio palatam ar gaiziara a.mazlumiSvilis


mosazreba imis Sesaxeb, rom mas sk-is 303-e muxlis me-2 nawilis Tanax-


mad, ufleba aqvs darCes binis damqiraveblad. saapelacio palatam


dadgenilad cno, rom miTiTebuli normiT gaTvaliswinebuli ufleba


mopasuxesa da misi ojaxis wevrebs ar gamouyenebiaT da ar aRuZravT


Segebebuli sarCeli. amasTan, saapelacio palatam CaTvala, rom sk-is


303-e muxlis me-2 nawili moqiravned darCenis uflebas aniWebs ipo-


TekiT datvirTul binaSi, mocemul SemTxvevaSi ki sadavo bina ar yo-


fila datvirTuli ipoTekiT.


saapelacio palatis ganCineba sakasacio wesiT gaasaCivra a. maz-


lumiSvilma. kasatori moiTxovs gasaCivrebuli gadawyvetilebis ga-


uqmebasa da axali gadawyvetilebiT sadavo binaSi damqiraveblad da-


tovebas. kasatori aRniSnavs, rom mas hqonda dayenebuli sasarCelo


moTxovna ojaxis wevrebTan erTad damqiraveblad datovebis Sesaxeb,


magram usafuZvlod eTqva uari.

mis masalebi da Tvlis, rom sakasacio saCivari ar unda dakmayofil-


des Semdeg garemoebaTa gamo:


dadgenilia, rom sadavo bina mosarCelem SeiZina sajaro auqcion-

sadavo bina ar yofila datvirTuli ipoTekiT. aRniSnuli faqtobri-

da dasabuTebul sakasacio pretenzias. saqmis masalebiT ar irkveva,


rom a.mazlumiSvilis mier sarCeli iyo aRZruli sadavo binaSi damqi-


raveblad darCenis moTxovniT. amasTan, sakasacio palata iziarebs
